}\n54:   void clearDynamicContextChanged() { dynamic_context_changed_ = false; }\n55:   bool dynamicContextChanged() const { return dynamic_context_changed_; }\n56: \n57:   void setControlPlaneIdentifier(const std::string& id) { control_plane_identifier_ = id; }\n58:   std::string& controlPlaneIdentifier() { return control_plane_identifier_; }\n59: \n60:   // Whether there was a change in our subscription interest we have yet to inform the server of.\n61:   virtual bool subscriptionUpdatePending() const PURE;\n62: \n63:   virtual void markStreamFresh() PURE;\n64: \n65:   UpdateAck handleResponse(const RS& response) {\n66:     // We *always* copy the response's nonce into the next request, even if we're going to make that\n67:     // request a NACK by setting error_detail.\n68:     UpdateAck ack(response.nonce(), typeUrl());\n69:     ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Handling response for {}\", typeUrl());\n70:     TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD { handleGoodResponse(response); }\n71:     END_TRY\n72:     catch (const EnvoyException& e) {\n73:       if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n74:         xds_config_tracker_->onConfigRejected(response,\n75:                                               Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n76:       }\n77:       handleBadResponse(e, ack);\n78:     }\n79:     previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n80:     return ack;\n81:   }\n82: \n83:   virtual void handleEstablishmentFailure() {\n84:     ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"SubscriptionState establishment failed for {}\", typeUrl());\n85:     callbacks().onConfigUpdateFailed(Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::ConnectionFailure,\n86:                                      nullptr);\n87:   }\n88: \n89:   // Returns the next gRPC request proto to be sent off to the server, based on this object's\n90:   // understanding of the current protocol state, and new resources that Envoy wants to request.\n91:   std::unique_ptr<RQ> getNextRequestAckless() { return getNextRequestInternal(); }\n92: \n93:   // The WithAck version first calls the ack-less version, then adds in the passed-in ack.\n94:   // Returns a new'd pointer, meant to be owned by the caller, who is expected to know what type the\n95:   // pointer actually is.\n96:   std::unique_ptr<RQ> getNextRequestWithAck(const UpdateAck& ack) {\n97:     auto request = getNextRequestInternal();\n98:     request->set_response_nonce(ack.nonce_);\n99:     ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"ACK for {} will have nonce {}\", typeUrl(), ack.nonce_);\n100:     if (ack.error_detail_.code() != Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Ok) {\n101:       // Don't needlessly make the field present-but-empty if status is ok.\n102:       request->mutable_error_detail()->CopyFrom(ack.error_detail_);\n103:     }\n104:     return request;\n105:   }\n106: \n107:   virtual void ttlExpiryCallback(const std::vector<std::string>& type_url) PURE;\n108: \n109: protected:\n110:   virtual std::unique_ptr<RQ> getNextRequestInternal() PURE;\n111:   virtual void handleGoodResponse(const RS& message) PURE;\n112:   void handleBadResponse(const EnvoyException& e, UpdateAck& ack) {\n113:     // Note that error_detail being set is what indicates that a (Delta)DiscoveryRequest is a NACK.\n114:     ack.error_detail_.set_code(Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Internal);\n115:     ack.error_detail_.set_message(Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n116:     ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Config for {} rejected: {}\", typeUrl(), e.what());\n117:     callbacks().onConfigUpdateFailed(Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::UpdateRejected, &e);\n118:   }\n119: \n120:   std::string typeUrl() const { return type_url_; gRPC Stream Handler (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/)\\n\\nThe **GrpcStream** class (grpc_stream.h) implements the low-level gRPC stream handling, managing bidirectional gRPC communication with backoff retry logic, rate limiting, and stream establishment/closure. It implements Grpc::AsyncStreamCallbacks and dispatches incoming DiscoveryResponse messages to the mux layer.\\n\\n## Legacy Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/)\\n\\nThe legacy implementation includes **GrpcMuxImpl** (grpc_mux_impl.h/cc) which manages subscriptions and multiplexes multiple resource types on a single ADS stream. The legacy delta-xDS variant tracks **DeltaSubscriptionState** (delta_subscription_state.h/cc), handling per-resource versioning and incremental updates. The legacy subscription layer (**GrpcSubscriptionImpl**, grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc) provides subscription management with factory patterns (grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc, grpc_collection_subscription_factory.h/cc).\\n\\n## New Unified Mux Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/)\\n\\nThe newer unified implementation provides template-based generic mux management with:\\n\\n- **GrpcMuxImpl** template (grpc_mux_impl.h/cc) - Generic mux managing subscriptions and request queuing\\n- **GrpcMuxDelta** - Delta-xDS specialization of GrpcMuxImpl\\n- **GrpcMuxSotw** - State-of-the-world (SotW) xDS specialization\\n- **BaseSubscriptionState** template (subscription_state.h) - Base protocol state tracker with ACK/NACK handling via **UpdateAck** struct\\n- **DeltaSubscriptionState** (delta_subscription_state.h/cc) - Tracks delta-xDS protocol state with per-resource version tracking (ResourceState) and incremental updates (names_added_, names_removed_)\\n- **SotwSubscriptionState** (sotw_subscription_state.h/cc) - Tracks state-of-the-world protocol state with full resource set management and version_info tracking\\n- **DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory** and **SotwSubscriptionStateFactory** - Create appropriate subscription state instances\\n\\n## Resource Subscription and ACK/NACK Processing\\n\\nResource subscription tracking is managed through:\\n\\n- **WatchMap** (watch_map.h/cc) - Maps resource name watches to subscription callbacks\\n- **PausableAckQueue** (pausable_ack_queue.h/cc) - Queues ACKs/NACKs with pause/resume capability for ordered delivery\\n- **UpdateAck** struct (update_ack.h) - Carries nonce, type_url, and error_detail for ACK/NACK handling\\n\\nThe ACK/NACK mechanism works by:\\n1. BaseSubscriptionState::handleResponse() copies the response nonce and marks errors in UpdateAck\\n2. getNextRequestWithAck() includes the nonce (ACK) and optional error_detail (NACK) in the next DiscoveryRequest\\n3. handleBadResponse() sets error_detail.code to Internal when validation fails, triggering a NACK\\n\\n## Additional Support Components\\n\\n- **GrpcMuxContext** (grpc_mux_context.h) - Configuration context for mux creation\\n- **GrpcMuxFailover** (grpc_mux_failover.h) - Failover support for primary/secondary xDS sources\\n- **EdsResourcesCacheImpl** (eds_resources_cache_impl.h/cc) - Caches EDS resources for optimization\\n- **XdsSourceId** (xds_source_id.h/cc) - Tracks xDS source identification\\n- **NewGrpcMuxImpl** (new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc) - Intermediate mux variant for migration\\n\\nThis architecture separates concerns: the GrpcStream handles transport-level gRPC operations, the mux manages resource subscriptions and request queuing, subscription states track protocol state and ACK/NACK logic, and the watch map manages application-level resource interest callbacks.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1662,"cache_read_input_tokens":91245,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1662},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0d5f73a7-15fc-4bdd-949f-3bca6210bb74","uuid":"c05dd4dd-8bd8-4bc5-95c3-833903e22007"}
